09/10/22, 10:54â€¯pm - Pratham singh Mait: Ans 4
09/10/22, 10:54â€¯pm - Pratham singh Mait: Hint for Question 4:


Let  the prize is behind a given door Ar, Ag,
and Ab.
To start  assume that we
have already picked the red door.
Let B "the presenter opens the green door". Without any
prior knowledge, assign this a probability of 50%
In  situation where the prize is behind the red door, he is free to pick between the green or the blue door at
random,  P(B | Ar) = 1 / 2

In situation where the prize is behind the green door, he must pick blue door P(B | Ag) = 0
In situation where the prize is behind the blue door, he must pick the green door, P(B | Ab) = 1
Thus,finally how this depends on the value of P(B)....

We're happy to open applications at the *Maharaja Agrasen Institute of Technology, Delhi* for the 2 month *Finlatics Financial Analyst program*, an *Online live project* that helps students *gain work experience* in *Financial Markets* and *Investment Banking*. The project is running at leading *campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Kanpur, DTU and BITS Pilani* among others.

Benefits post completion: 
1. *Certificate of Work  Experience*
2. *Letter of Recommendation*. The project includes *personalized mentoring* interactions for financial markets guidance and *live sessions* for investment banking.
3. *Incentives* : upto Rs. 6000 (for top performers) 

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we will get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/pevc_combo/application/index.php?utm_src=maitw

*Project start*: Flexible on student choice

*Project Breaks*: Selected students will be eligible for a break during the project if they need it for any exams, assignments, or personal commitments. 

*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge are required to be a part of this project

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee: Rs. 1499 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST (on student choice)

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

17/01/23, 1:34â€¯pm - Asmi O1 Mait: This message was deleted
17/01/23, 1:34â€¯pm - Asmi O1 Mait: Dear Students,
 
Welcome to Career Development Cell!
 
 Namankan is the First Step for enrolling services of our Cell which is not at all limited to Placement or Internships but also includes Higher Studies, Entrepreneurship, Start Ups, GATE Preparation, Gov. Job Preparations and similar Career related Activities, which further extended to the domain of Alumni Network for Job Referrals even after you being passed out.
 
Every Student is hereby mandated for Obligatory registration via this form.
 
Find the Link to the Namankan form:
https://forms.gle/UALoBgkvEe6f67z47

 
This form is further processed to validate your credentials and to form Master Datasheets (MDS) of respective passing out years. We denominate each Sheet in the format with a name, for example, MDS 2025 which reflects the Master datasheet of all the students from all the branches who are going to pass out in 2025. Any Migration admission, Lateral Entry, Year Back Case or Diploma Student is equivalent only if they are being passed out in the same year, here 2022.
 
After the formation of MDS, we use the data to form google groups and Invitation to our Whatsapp Student Care Groups.
 
We use MDS, to enrol you for various Corporate Actions, Registrations, Internships, Placements, Events and competitions. This is not at all limited to placements and internships but for Alumni and even for your Student/ Alumni Credential Verifications after you passed out where Various Companies, Organizations, Government Jobs, and Visas seek our confirmation for the same.
 
You must adhere to our Terms and  Conditions as stated or communicated based on requirements.
In general, You must always entertain our emails, respond to the needful actions and can seek help using Provided email addresses and Whatsapp Student Care groups.
In any case, you must not share our emails or correspondence with anyone outside MAIT esp. for placement & Internship Drives. This not just only impacts you but everyone in our MAIT Student Community as this will decrease your and your peer's chance of Recruitment.
If you happen to get any HR contact details from our Emails or by any platform, must not be shared even among your fast/ Best friends and acquaintances or utilized or abused in any way.
You must not Correspond to any Corporate, or HR directly even in urgency. Every communication must be routed through us to safeguard the interests of every stakeholder in this regard.
You will not decline any offer from any company without discussing it with us otherwise this will impact your peers and juniors in the forthcoming days.
Students are free to opt for any company or option provided they consult with us and adhere to our instructions.
We have various ways and tacts to settle these issues. We train you also in handling these situations. So we vary this and be part of our KAIZEN program.
Students can contact us using our Email ID only. In any case, you must not try to use any informal way like Whatsapp or Mobile Conversations.
To help you, the First mode of contact is the Whatsapp Student Care group where CDC Coordinators are appointed to sort your enquiries.
As a last resort, you can escalate the matter directly to us using email only. And wait for a response. We try our best to respond as soon as possible but sufficient time must be given. We could only respond if we have the requisite info, otherwise, we also escalate with the respective Authority/ HR/ Company. You must have patience.
In any case, we do not accept Unprofessional or Casual email Ids. We already have informed you to get email addresses properly as per our prior instructions.
We do not change email IDs & Primary Mobile Numbers and will discourage you to adhere with it for all CDC-related activities esp. with Recruitment and Internship Drives.
 
You must always double-check any information that you feed in Namankan form or other Requisitions with all validity, honesty and integrity. Any misled in any data form or communication will certainly invite Disciplinary action. This will reflect in your Character Certifications and Internal Student Audit Reports which we share with your prospective employers whether for Campus Drives or Off Campus drives or Even you being passed out after, let's say 10 years. You must take this Sincerely and seriously. Even Green Card Holders are being validated by us.
 
We encourage vigilant students to report misconduct by anyone in any case. We won't disclose their identity or penalize them but instead, reward them for their Proactiveness. So, if you come across any glitch or issue, you must report it to us on an immediate basis.
 
Students have the right to inform us of any misinformation especially with Data related to MDS, for which we try to give open access among students as and when required. Which not only contains Academic information but their Discipline Status, Participation in Placement and Cell activities.

Complete the task asap with full accuracy.
Any misinformation will make you ineligible for all future drives hence accuracy and precision lie on your shoulders.
If you have 69.99 % then mark it 69.99%, you are not allowed to do even a .01% of deviation. Yes, 69.987% could be written as 69.99% but beyond this, No Rounding off is allowed. Every student is marked Unverified as we have not seen your originals. We conduct a verification process for the same.

  A few more instructions are as:  

1. Those who don't have B.Tech. Aggregate available like Second Year Lateral Entry must mark '11' just to complete the form for B.Tech. Aggregate Percentage. 

2. All others must calculate their percentages very carefully.

3. If you have a backlog then do not include that subject while calculating B.Tech. Aggregate.

4. Unless you have announced & Published Backlog Subjects results for your backlogs, mark them as it is. You have to give a count of your backlogs in the 3 categories as mentioned in the form.

5. For 10th, 12th, & Diploma Aggregate marks must be as it is, as mentioned on mark sheets.      
If not then you have to take the simple arithmetic mean of all the subjects enlisted in mark sheets. There is no rule of Top Five or Top 4 subject counts with Corporates. They count every subject you have on Marksheets.

6. When asked for CGPA, then mark CGPA in respective places and When a percentage is asked esp. with 10th, then Do not mark CGPA. Conversion from CGPA into Percentage or vice-versa must be followed as per criteria printed on the mark sheets only. No whimsical figure could be used. 

7. In any case, for B.Tech. results refer only to your mark sheets issued by University or the Published Result PDF on University's website. Do not refer to any other third-party website or Application to calculate the percentages. Do the Math yourself as many times these Websites give erroneous results esp when the backlog is there or migration or Lateral Admission or Shift in Branch or Upgradation happens.

Breach of trust, in any case, will result in the cancellation of your offer or placement candidature for all future drives.
Please be very careful, vigilant and honest about every word and document related to this form.

Students can edit the form if new updated information is available or if they are not added to any of the CDC Whatsapp/email groups.

Are you ready to witness the magic of Nucleya at Rendezvous'23? The trailblazer of the Indian bass music scene is all set to take over our stage and mesmerize us with his unique fusion of Indian melodies, rhythms, and bass-heavy electronic music. Nucleya has made his mark as one of India's most popular and influential independent artists, with his sound being a genre in itself that has inspired a wave of desi bass producers.

From his debut EP "Koocha Monster" to his latest collaboration with Ritviz on the EP "Baaraat," He has consistently produced anthems that have become the soundtrack of a new Indian generation - frenetic, loud, and unabashedly Indian. But that's not all. He has also shared the stage with global bass stars such as Skrillex, Major Lazer, DJ Snake, Krewella, and Flux Pavilion. 

Don't miss out on this unforgettable performance that is sure to leave you mesmerized!

We're pleased to open applications at *Maharaja Agrasen Institute of Technology* for the Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program, an *Online Live Project* that helps students gain *Work Experience* in *Data-driven decision-making*.

The project uses a case study-driven approach, where you will assess business projects and solve problems using models used by leading firms like *Accenture, Capgemini & Cognizant*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on *real business data* to gain insights.

The project is running in leading campuses like *IIT Delhi, IIT Kanpur, IIT Bombay*, and *BITS Pilani*.

At the end of this program, you will get: 
- *Certificate of Work Experience*
- *Letter of Recommendation* on performance

To apply, you can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba/application/index.php?utm_src=maitw

*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of this project. 

*Project Duration*: 1 month / 2 months (on your choice)

*Project Start*: Flexible on your schedule. 

You can also take a *break* for exams, assignments, or personal commitments as well as take an *extension* if you cannot complete it within the duration. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs.1999 + GST

*Fee Waiver*:  A *fee waiver* of *25%* shall be given to all *MAIT* students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will reduce the fee to Rs. 1499 + GST.

Team Finlatics
